            });
          });

          // Unregister the legacy OneSignal service worker to prevent scope conflicts
          if (navigator.serviceWorker) {
            navigator.serviceWorker.getRegistrations().then((registrations) => {
              // Iterate through all registered service workers
              registrations.forEach((registration) => {
                // Check the script URL to identify the specific service worker
                if (registration.active && registration.active.scriptURL.includes('OneSignalSDKWorker.js.php')) {
                  // Unregister the service worker
                  registration.unregister().then((success) => {
                    if (success) {
                      console.log('OneSignalSW: Successfully unregistered:', registration.active.scriptURL);
                    } else {
                      console.log('OneSignalSW: Failed to unregister:', registration.active.scriptURL);
                    }
                  });
                }
              });
            }).catch((error) => {
              console.error('Error fetching service worker registrations:', error);
            });

    	<script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/moment.js/2.30.1/moment.min.js"></script>
	<script>
		const today = moment().format("dddd DD MMM").toString().toUpperCase();
		//console.log("today", today);
        const dayLists = document.querySelectorAll('.schedule-day');
        const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.schedule-content');
        const prevBtn = document.getElementById('schedule-prev');
        const nextBtn = document.getElementById('schedule-next');
		
		jQuery(document).ready(function() {
			// Wrap time with span.listTime and remaining content with span.listContent
			jQuery('.schedule-content ul li').each(function() {
				let text = jQuery(this).text();
				let time = text.split(' ')[0];
				let content = text.replace(time, '').trim();
				jQuery(this).html(`<span class="listTime">${time}</span> <span class="listContent">${content}</span>`);
			});
		});

        function updateVisibility() {            
            dayLists.forEach(dayList => {
                const date = dayList.getAttribute('data-fullday');
                //console.log('Date', date)
				if (date === today) {
                    dayList.classList.add('active');
				} else {
					dayList.classList.remove('active');
				}
            });

            contents.forEach(content => {
                const date = content.getAttribute('data-fullday');
                //console.log(date)
                if (date === today) {
                    content.classList.add('active');
                } else {
                    content.classList.remove('active');
                }
            });
        }

        prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            let currentActiveIndex = Array.from(dayLists).findIndex(dayList => dayList.classList.contains('active'));
            let currentContentActiveIndex = Array.from(contents).findIndex(content => content.classList.contains('active'));
            dayLists[currentActiveIndex].classList.remove('active');
            contents[currentContentActiveIndex].classList.remove('active');
            let prevIndex = currentActiveIndex === 0 ? dayLists.length - 1 : currentActiveIndex - 1;
            let contentPrevIndex = currentContentActiveIndex === 0 ? contents.length - 1 : currentContentActiveIndex - 1;
            dayLists[prevIndex].classList.add('active');
            contents[contentPrevIndex].classList.add('active');
			
			scrollToHighlighted();
        });

        nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            let currentActiveIndex = Array.from(dayLists).findIndex(dayList => dayList.classList.contains('active'));
            let currentContentActiveIndex = Array.from(contents).findIndex(content => content.classList.contains('active'));
            dayLists[currentActiveIndex].classList.remove('active');
            contents[currentContentActiveIndex].classList.remove('active');
            let nextIndex = currentActiveIndex === dayLists.length - 1 ? 0 : currentActiveIndex + 1;
            let contentNextIndex = currentContentActiveIndex === contents.length - 1 ? 0 : currentContentActiveIndex + 1;
            dayLists[nextIndex].classList.add('active');
            contents[contentNextIndex].classList.add('active');
			
			scrollToHighlighted()
        });

        updateVisibility(); // Initial visibility update
        // Add highlight
        addHighLight();
        // Set interval to check for time every 1 sec
        setInterval(addHighLight, 1000)
		//scroll to highlighted
// 		scrollToHighlighted()
		
		window.addEventListener('load', function () {
			// Get the highlighted element
			var highlightedElement = document.querySelector(".highlighted");

			// Check if the highlighted element exists
			if (highlightedElement) {
				// Scroll the .schedule-content div to the highlighted element's position
				var scheduleContent = document.querySelector(".schedule-list-wrapper");
				scheduleContent.scrollTop = highlightedElement.offsetTop - scheduleContent.offsetTop;
			}
		});	

        function addHighLight() {
            // Get the current date
            const currentDate = moment().format("dddd DD MMM");

            // Get all schedule content elements
            const scheduleContents = document.querySelectorAll('.schedule-content');

            // Loop through each schedule content element
            scheduleContents.forEach(scheduleContent => {
                // Extract the full day from the data attribute
                const fullDay = scheduleContent.getAttribute('data-fullday');

                // Check if the full day is equal to today's date
                if (fullDay === today) {
                    // Get the corresponding list element
                    const scheduleList = scheduleContent.querySelector('.schedule');

                    // Get the current time
                    const currentTime = moment();

                    // Remove highlight from any previously highlighted items
                    const highlightedItems = scheduleList.getElementsByClassName('highlighted');
                    while (highlightedItems.length > 0) {
                        highlightedItems[0].classList.remove('highlighted');
                    }

                    // Initialize variables to store the nearest time and its corresponding list item
                    let nearestTimeDiff = Infinity;
                    let nearestListItem = null;

					// Get all list items
					const listItems = scheduleList.querySelectorAll('li');    
					// Loop through each list item
					listItems.forEach((listItem) => {
						// Get the listTime element within the list item
						const listTimeElement = listItem.querySelector('.listTime');

						// Check if the listTime element exists
						if (listTimeElement) {
							// Extract the time from the listTime element
							const listItemTime = moment(listTimeElement.textContent, "HH:mm");

							// Check if the list item's time is not in the future compared to the current time
							if (listItemTime.isSameOrBefore(currentTime)) {
								// Calculate the difference in minutes between the current time and the list item's time
								const timeDiff = Math.abs(currentTime.diff(listItemTime, 'minutes'));

								// Check if this item's time is closer than the previous nearest time
								if (timeDiff < nearestTimeDiff) {
									nearestTimeDiff = timeDiff;
									nearestListItem = listItem;
								}
							}
						}
					});

                    // Apply the CSS class to highlight the nearest list item
                    if (nearestListItem) {
                        nearestListItem.classList.add('highlighted');
                    }
                }
            });

        }

    	<script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/moment.js/2.30.1/moment.min.js"></script>
	<script>
		const sukma_today = moment().format("dddd DD MMM").toString().toUpperCase();
		console.log("today", sukma_today);
        const sukma_dayLists = document.querySelectorAll('.sukma-schedule-day');
        const sukma_contents = document.querySelectorAll('.sukma-schedule-content');
        const sukma_prevBtn = document.getElementById('sukma-schedule-prev');
        const sukma_nextBtn = document.getElementById('sukma-schedule-next');
		
		jQuery(document).ready(function() {
			// Wrap time with span.listTime and remaining content with span.listContent
			jQuery('.sukma-schedule-content ul li').each(function() {
				let sukma_text = jQuery(this).text();
				let sukma_time = sukma_text.split(' ')[0];
				let sukma_content = sukma_text.replace(sukma_time, '').trim();
				jQuery(this).html(`<span class="sukma-listTime">${sukma_time}</span> <span class="sukma-listContent">${sukma_content}</span>`);
			});
		});

        function sukma_updateVisibility() {            
            sukma_dayLists.forEach(sukma_dayList => {
                const sukma_date = sukma_dayList.getAttribute('data-sukma-fullday');
                //console.log('Date', date)
				if (sukma_date === sukma_today) {
                    sukma_dayList.classList.add('sukma-active');
				} else {
					sukma_dayList.classList.remove('sukma-active');
				}
            });

            sukma_contents.forEach(sukma_content => {
                const sukma_date = sukma_content.getAttribute('data-sukma-fullday');
                //console.log(date)
                if (sukma_date === sukma_today) {
                    sukma_content.classList.add('sukma-active');
                } else {
                    sukma_content.classList.remove('sukma-active');
                }
            });
        }

        sukma_prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            let sukma_currentActiveIndex = Array.from(sukma_dayLists).findIndex(sukma_dayList => sukma_dayList.classList.contains('sukma-active'));
            let sukma_currentContentActiveIndex = Array.from(sukma_contents).findIndex(sukma_content => sukma_content.classList.contains('sukma-active'));
            sukma_dayLists[sukma_currentActiveIndex].classList.remove('sukma-active');
            sukma_contents[sukma_currentContentActiveIndex].classList.remove('sukma-active');
            let sukma_prevIndex = sukma_currentActiveIndex === 0 ? sukma_dayLists.length - 1 : sukma_currentActiveIndex - 1;
            let sukma_contentPrevIndex = sukma_currentContentActiveIndex === 0 ? sukma_contents.length - 1 : sukma_currentContentActiveIndex - 1;
            sukma_dayLists[sukma_prevIndex].classList.add('sukma-active');
            sukma_contents[sukma_contentPrevIndex].classList.add('sukma-active');
			
			//sukma_scrollToHighlighted();
        });

        sukma_nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            let sukma_currentActiveIndex = Array.from(sukma_dayLists).findIndex(sukma_dayList => sukma_dayList.classList.contains('sukma-active'));
            let sukma_currentContentActiveIndex = Array.from(sukma_contents).findIndex(sukma_content => sukma_content.classList.contains('sukma-active'));
            sukma_dayLists[sukma_currentActiveIndex].classList.remove('sukma-active');
            sukma_contents[sukma_currentContentActiveIndex].classList.remove('sukma-active');
            let sukma_nextIndex = sukma_currentActiveIndex === sukma_dayLists.length - 1 ? 0 : sukma_currentActiveIndex + 1;
            let sukma_contentNextIndex = sukma_currentContentActiveIndex === sukma_contents.length - 1 ? 0 : sukma_currentContentActiveIndex + 1;
            sukma_dayLists[sukma_nextIndex].classList.add('sukma-active');
            sukma_contents[sukma_contentNextIndex].classList.add('sukma-active');
			
			//scrollToHighlighted()
        });

        sukma_updateVisibility(); // Initial visibility update
        // Add highlight
        sukma_addHighLight();
        // Set interval to check for time every 1 sec
        setInterval(sukma_addHighLight, 1000)
		//scroll to highlighted
// 		scrollToHighlighted()
		
		window.addEventListener('load', function () {
			// Get the highlighted element
			var sukma_highlightedElement = document.querySelector(".sukma-highlighted");

			// Check if the highlighted element exists
			if (sukma_highlightedElement) {
				// Scroll the .schedule-content div to the highlighted element's position
				var sukma_scheduleContent = document.querySelector(".sukma-schedule-list-wrapper");
				sukma_scheduleContent.scrollTop = sukma_highlightedElement.offsetTop - sukma_scheduleContent.offsetTop;
			}
		});	

        function sukma_addHighLight() {
            // Get the current date
            const sukma_currentDate = moment().format("dddd DD MMM");

            // Get all schedule content elements
            const sukma_scheduleContents = document.querySelectorAll('.sukma-schedule-content');

            // Loop through each schedule content element
            sukma_scheduleContents.forEach(sukma_scheduleContent => {
                // Extract the full day from the data attribute
                const sukma_fullDay = sukma_scheduleContent.getAttribute('data-sukma-fullday');

                // Check if the full day is equal to today's date
                if (sukma_fullDay === sukma_today) {
                    // Get the corresponding list element
                    const sukma_scheduleList = sukma_scheduleContent.querySelector('.sukma-schedule');

                    // Get the current time
                    const sukma_currentTime = moment();

                    // Remove highlight from any previously highlighted items
                    const sukma_highlightedItems = sukma_scheduleList.getElementsByClassName('sukma-highlighted');
                    while (sukma_highlightedItems.length > 0) {
                        sukma_highlightedItems[0].classList.remove('sukma-highlighted');
                    }

                    // Initialize variables to store the nearest time and its corresponding list item
                    let sukma_nearestTimeDiff = Infinity;
                    let sukma_nearestListItem = null;

					// Get all list items
					const sukma_listItems = sukma_scheduleList.querySelectorAll('li');    
					// Loop through each list item
					sukma_listItems.forEach((sukma_listItem) => {
						// Get the listTime element within the list item
						const sukma_listTimeElement = sukma_listItem.querySelector('.sukma-listTime');

						// Check if the listTime element exists
						if (sukma_listTimeElement) {
							// Extract the time from the listTime element
							const sukma_listItemTime = moment(sukma_listTimeElement.textContent, "HH:mm");

							// Check if the list item's time is not in the future compared to the current time
							if (sukma_listItemTime.isSameOrBefore(sukma_currentTime)) {
								// Calculate the difference in minutes between the current time and the list item's time
								const sukma_timeDiff = Math.abs(sukma_currentTime.diff(sukma_listItemTime, 'minutes'));

								// Check if this item's time is closer than the previous nearest time
								if (sukma_timeDiff < sukma_nearestTimeDiff) {
									sukma_nearestTimeDiff = sukma_timeDiff;
									sukma_nearestListItem = sukma_listItem;
								}
							}
						}
					});

                    // Apply the CSS class to highlight the nearest list item
                    if (sukma_nearestListItem) {
                        sukma_nearestListItem.classList.add('sukma-highlighted');
                    }
                }
            });

        }
		
// 		function scrollToHighlighted(){

    </script>
    </div>
</div>
						</div>
				</div>
				</div>
					</div>

	<span class="cff-text" data-color="">Ketua jurulatih Kuching City FC, Aidil Sharin Sahak optimis perebutan tempat kedua Liga Super masih terbuka biarpun pasukannya kini menghuni tangga keempat carta Liga Super.<br /><br />Pengendali dari Singapura itu berkata, meskipun Kuala Lumpur City FC telah memintas pasukannya dengan kelebihan dua mata, namun situasi itu tidak merencatkan keyakinan beliau bahawa saingan kelompok tiga teratas masih belum muktamad.<br /><br />Baca berita penuh: <a href="https://www.tvsarawak.my/2026/02/23/perebutan-tempat-kedua-liga-super-masih-terbuka-aidil-sharin-sahak/">www.tvsarawak.my/2026/02/23/perebutan-tempat-kedua-liga-super-masih-terbuka-aidil-sharin-sahak/</a> 	</span>

	<span class="cff-text" data-color="">Rang Undang-Undang Perlembagaan (Pindaan) 2026 berkaitan had tempoh jawatan Perdana Menteri akan mengambil kira tempoh perkhidmatan terdahulu individu yang pernah memegang jawatan itu.<br /><br />Menteri di Jabatan Perdana Menteri (Undang-Undang dan Reformasi Institusi) Datuk Seri Azalina Othman Said berkata, had maksimum 10 tahun yang dicadangkan menerusi pindaan perlembagaan itu bukan sahaja terpakai bagi tempoh perkhidmatan selepas ia berkuat kuasa, malah merangkumi tempoh terdahulu seseorang yang pernah menjadi Perdana Menteri.<br /><br />Baca artikel penuh: <a href="https://www.tvsarawak.my/2026/02/23/had-tempoh-jawatan-perdana-menteri-ambil-kira-perkhidmatan-lalu/">www.tvsarawak.my/2026/02/23/had-tempoh-jawatan-perdana-menteri-ambil-kira-perkhidmatan-lalu/</a> 	</span>

				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );

			<style type="text/css" data-ctf-style="3">.ctf-feed-3 .ctf-tweet-text, .ctf-feed-3 .ctf-quoted-tweet-text{font-size:14px!important;}.ctf-feed-3 .ctf-tweet-actions a{font-size:12px!important;}.ctf-feed-3 .ctf-twitterlink{font-size:9px!important;}.ctf-feed-3 .ctf-tweet-text a{color:#27a5a0!important;}.ctf-feed-3.ctf-regular-style .ctf-item, .ctf-feed-3 .ctf-header{border-bottom:1px solid #DDD!important;}.ctf-feed-3.ctf_palette_custom_3 .ctf-item, .ctf-feed-3.ctf_palette_custom_3 .ctf-header{background:#FFFFFF!important;}</style><script type="text/javascript">
		/* MonsterInsights Scroll Tracking */
			if ( typeof(jQuery) !== 'undefined' ) {
				jQuery( document ).ready(function(){
					function monsterinsights_scroll_tracking_load() {
						if ( ( typeof(__gaTracker) !== 'undefined' && __gaTracker && __gaTracker.hasOwnProperty( "loaded" ) && __gaTracker.loaded == true ) || ( typeof(__gtagTracker) !== 'undefined' && __gtagTracker ) ) {
							(function(factory) {
								factory(jQuery);
							}(function($) {

								/* Scroll Depth */
								"use strict";
								var defaults = {
									percentage: true
								};

								var $window = $(window),
									cache = [],
									scrollEventBound = false,
									lastPixelDepth = 0;

								/*
								 * Plugin
								 */

								$.scrollDepth = function(options) {

									var startTime = +new Date();

									options = $.extend({}, defaults, options);

									/*
									 * Functions
									 */

									function sendEvent(action, label, scrollDistance, timing) {
										if ( 'undefined' === typeof MonsterInsightsObject || 'undefined' === typeof MonsterInsightsObject.sendEvent ) {
											return;
										}
											var paramName = action.toLowerCase();
	var fieldsArray = {
		send_to: 'G-K6RTN3E4NH',
		non_interaction: true
	};
	fieldsArray[paramName] = label;

	if (arguments.length > 3) {
		fieldsArray.scroll_timing = timing
		MonsterInsightsObject.sendEvent('event', 'scroll_depth', fieldsArray);
	} else {
		MonsterInsightsObject.sendEvent('event', 'scroll_depth', fieldsArray);
	}
										}

									function calculateMarks(docHeight) {
										return {
											'25%' : parseInt(docHeight * 0.25, 10),
											'50%' : parseInt(docHeight * 0.50, 10),
											'75%' : parseInt(docHeight * 0.75, 10),
											/* Cushion to trigger 100% event in iOS */
											'100%': docHeight - 5
										};
									}

									function checkMarks(marks, scrollDistance, timing) {
										/* Check each active mark */
										$.each(marks, function(key, val) {
											if ( $.inArray(key, cache) === -1 && scrollDistance >= val ) {
												sendEvent('Percentage', key, scrollDistance, timing);
												cache.push(key);
											}
										});
									}

									function rounded(scrollDistance) {
										/* Returns String */
										return (Math.floor(scrollDistance/250) * 250).toString();
									}

									function init() {
										bindScrollDepth();
									}

									/*
									 * Public Methods
									 */

									/* Reset Scroll Depth with the originally initialized options */
									$.scrollDepth.reset = function() {
										cache = [];
										lastPixelDepth = 0;
										$window.off('scroll.scrollDepth');
										bindScrollDepth();
									};

									/* Add DOM elements to be tracked */
									$.scrollDepth.addElements = function(elems) {

										if (typeof elems == "undefined" || !$.isArray(elems)) {
											return;
										}

										$.merge(options.elements, elems);

										/* If scroll event has been unbound from window, rebind */
										if (!scrollEventBound) {
											bindScrollDepth();
										}

									};

									/* Remove DOM elements currently tracked */
									$.scrollDepth.removeElements = function(elems) {

										if (typeof elems == "undefined" || !$.isArray(elems)) {
											return;
										}

										$.each(elems, function(index, elem) {

											var inElementsArray = $.inArray(elem, options.elements);
											var inCacheArray = $.inArray(elem, cache);

											if (inElementsArray != -1) {
												options.elements.splice(inElementsArray, 1);
											}

											if (inCacheArray != -1) {
												cache.splice(inCacheArray, 1);
											}

										});

									};

									/*
									 * Throttle function borrowed from:
									 * Underscore.js 1.5.2
									 * http://underscorejs.org
									 * (c) 2009-2013 Jeremy Ashkenas, DocumentCloud and Investigative Reporters & Editors
									 * Underscore may be freely distributed under the MIT license.
									 */

									function throttle(func, wait) {
										var context, args, result;
										var timeout = null;
										var previous = 0;
										var later = function() {
											previous = new Date;
											timeout = null;
											result = func.apply(context, args);
										};
										return function() {
											var now = new Date;
											if (!previous) previous = now;
											var remaining = wait - (now - previous);
											context = this;
											args = arguments;
											if (remaining <= 0) {
												clearTimeout(timeout);
												timeout = null;
												previous = now;
												result = func.apply(context, args);
											} else if (!timeout) {
												timeout = setTimeout(later, remaining);
											}
											return result;
										};
									}

									/*
									 * Scroll Event
									 */

									function bindScrollDepth() {

										scrollEventBound = true;

										$window.on('scroll.scrollDepth', throttle(function() {
											/*
											 * We calculate document and window height on each scroll event to
											 * account for dynamic DOM changes.
											 */

											var docHeight = $(document).height(),
												winHeight = window.innerHeight ? window.innerHeight : $window.height(),
												scrollDistance = $window.scrollTop() + winHeight,

												/* Recalculate percentage marks */
												marks = calculateMarks(docHeight),

												/* Timing */
												timing = +new Date - startTime;

											checkMarks(marks, scrollDistance, timing);
										}, 500));

									}

									init();
								};

								/* UMD export */
								return $.scrollDepth;

							}));

							jQuery.scrollDepth();
						} else {
							setTimeout(monsterinsights_scroll_tracking_load, 200);
						}
					}
					monsterinsights_scroll_tracking_load();
				});
			}
		/* End MonsterInsights Scroll Tracking */

<!-- Back to top button -->
<a id="to-top"></a>
			
<script>
(function($){
	var btn = $('#to-top');
	var mobBtn = $('#back-to-top');

	if($(window).width() <= 680){
		mobBtn.on('click', function(e) {
		  e.preventDefault();
		  $('html, body').animate({scrollTop:0}, '300');
		});
	} else {
		$(window).scroll(function() {
		  if ($(window).scrollTop() > 300) {
			btn.addClass('show');
		  } else {
			btn.removeClass('show');
		  }
		});
		btn.on('click', function(e) {
		  e.preventDefault();
		  $('html, body').animate({scrollTop:0}, '300');
		});
	}
	
})(jQuery)
</script>
